- **17063**: Set starting pattern? [[/$26] Random (A-E)./[/$26] Pattern A./[/$26] Pattern B./[/$26] Pattern C./[/$26] Pattern D./[/$26] Pattern E./No thanks.]
- **17064**: Starting pattern set to [Random/Pattern A/Pattern B/Pattern C/Pattern D/Pattern E].
- **17065**: Set starting player? [[/$26] Random./[/$26] You./[/$26] Opponent./No thanks.]
- **17066**: Starting player set to [Random/You/Opponent].
- **17067**: Read the manual? [Sure./No thanks.]
- **17068**: Mandragora Mania is a game in which you battle for jingly by moving your mandragora pieces to the goal.
- **17069**: Your goal is the [red/blue/green] one on the right, while your opponent's is the [blue/green/red] one on the left.
- **17070**: At the start of the game, three mandragoras each will be placed on the eight game areas, excluding the goal.
- **17071**: There are five starting placements (A through E), and you are able to select which one you would like to employ. The default setting is "Random."
- **17072**: This explanation uses pattern A, but the basic rules are the same regardless of the starting pattern.
- **17073**: The three [red/blue/green] areas in front of you are yours,the three [blue/green/red] areas at the back are your opponent's,and the remaining two are neutral.
- **17074**: You must choose one area--either yours or a neutral one--to proceed.
- **17075**: The areas are numbered from one to five starting from the left, and any mandragoras in the area you select will move.
- **17076**: Conversely, your opponent must select either a neutral area or an area that belongs to them.
- **17077**: From the right, those areas are numbered 6, 4, 7, 2, and 8.
- **17078**: For example, if you select Area 1,one mandragora will move to Area 2and one will move to Area 3,and one will move to Area 4.
- **17079**: Note that the mandragoras will move from the back first--last in, first out.
- **17080**: You will receive points known as "jingly" each time one of your mandragoras reaches the goal.
- **17081**: You will enter your opponent's territory whenever you go past the goal.
- **17082**: If one of your mandragoras happens to reach the opponent's goal, the goal will be pushed back and your mandragora will return to your own area. You don't have to worry about your mandragora earning any jingly for your opponent.
- **17083**: The order in which players choose areas will be determined based on your turn settings. The default setting is random.
- **17084**: This explanation has skipped past your opponent's turn for demonstration purposes, but in the actual game you and your opponent will take turns choosing areas.
- **17085**: However, if the last mandragora to move reaches the goal, you will get to take an additional turn.
- **17086**: Mandragoras are a very diverse species, and the amount of jingly you earn is determined by the species of mandragora that crosses into the goal.
- **17087**: Adenium and citrullus: 3 jingly (first player)/4 jingly (second player).
- **17088**: Korrigan and pachypodium: 2 jingly (first player)/3 jingly (second player).
- **17089**: Standard mandragoras: 1 jingly (both players).
- **17090**: The game is over when either you or your opponent no longer has any mandragoras that can move.
- **17091**: The player who has the most jingly at that point will be declared the winner.
- **17092**: The key to victory lies in taking advantage of the various mandragora subspecies bonuses while claiming multiple turns in a row.
- **17093**: $7$7$7$7$7 Pattern [A/B/C/D/E] - Your Turn ([First Player/Second Player]) $7$7$7$7$7
- **17094**: You have selected Area $0.
